> _Prior:_ 2026-07-05 by **PP-B3 RESOLVED — 5 attributes were emitted in the WRONG PP Appendix A datatype → LIVE `main` + Staging**. The audit's highest-priority open item (potential PP106 whole-listing rejection) was settled with a **read-only `GetFullDetailsOfAllListingsByBranch` call against the live HFC branch (327 listings)** — the authoritative datatype ground truth. Result: `Kitchen`(191/191 stored `"Yes"`), `Family_TV_Room`(11), `Study`(13), `StaffQuarters`(16), `Entrance_hall`(37) are all **boolean `"Yes"`** in Appendix A, but `PrivatePropertyListingMapper::buildAttributes()` emitted them as **integer counts** in the `$counts` loop — a datatype mismatch. **Why it never visibly broke:** PP *coerces* a numeric value to `"Yes"` for boolean attributes (the ONLY reason property 6049 survived with `Kitchen="1"` — the audit's "Kitchen is a proven count" anchor was WRONG; PP silently coerced it). The 2026-07-02 PP106s were the *reverse* mismatch (old `EnSuite="true"` boolean → integer attr, since fixed to `EnSuite="1"`). **Fix:** the five moved out of `$counts` into present-only `"Yes"` flags (keyed off `Kitchen`/`TV Room`/`Study`+`Office`/`Domestic Room`/`Entrance Hall` spaces); `Lounges`/`DiningAreas`/`Parking`/`Carports` stay integer counts (read-back-confirmed 1–3). Tinker-verified: buildAttributes now emits Kitchen/Family_TV_Room/Study/StaffQuarters/Entrance_hall=`"Yes"`, Lounges/DiningAreas/Parking/Carports=int. `GetFullDetailsOfAllListingsByBranch` is the standard read-back to settle any future count-vs-flag question (WSDL op exists; called via the client's generic `call()`). Files: `PrivatePropertyListingMapper.php`, audit doc (PP-B3 → RESOLVED). No migration/route/perm. ⚠️ live box is `--no-dev` → run `PpFeatureAttributesTest` on laragon.
>
> _Prior:_ 2026-07-05 by **SYNDICATION MAPPING FIXES (5) → LIVE `main` + Staging**. From the 2026-07-05 syndication-mapping audit (`.ai/audits/syndication-mapping-audit-2026-07-05.md`), the five confirmed "fix-now" items landed. **PP (`PrivatePropertyListingMapper`):** (PP-B1) `Carports` was dead code — `countSpaces($property,'Carport')` but a carport is a FEATURE of the `Parking` space, not a space type, so it always returned 0 and never syndicated → new `countCarports()` sums Parking bays/units carrying the `Carport` feature (space-level featuresAll ⇒ bay count, else per-unit hits; tinker-proven 2/2/0). (PP-B2) `Laundry` checked `hasSpace('Laundry')` but the space type is `'Laundry Room'` → never fired → fixed. (PP-G1) seven amenity flags (Gym/Clubhouse/TennisCourt/SquashCourt/Jaccuzzi/Jetty_Berth/Storage) only checked `has()` feature strings, so entered as a SPACE they never fired → OR-ed the matching `hasSpace(<type>)` (Gym/Clubhouse/Tennis Court/Squash Court/Jacuzzi/Jetty/Storeroom, all verified against `config/property-spaces.php`). **P24 (`Property24ListingMapper`):** (P24-B1) `showLocation` used `(bool)($lat && $lng)` but lat/lng are `decimal:7` string casts ("0.0000000" is truthy) → never-geocoded listings emitted `showLocation:true` (privacy-adjacent) → numeric guard mirroring the proven line-82 `geographicLocation` fix. (P24-G1) `rentalInfo.rentalRate` never sent → weekly/daily/short-term rentals published at P24's default MONTHLY cadence → new `mapRentalRate()` maps `rental_price_type` → RentalRate enum (Month/Week/Day/Year/SquareMetre), NULL for blank/unknown so P24 keeps its own default. ⚠️ LIVE `/corex` box is `composer install --no-dev` (no phpunit) → verification was `php -l`-clean + a bootstrapped tinker harness (Carports both shapes, all 8 space strings resolve, every rental cadence maps); the covering test files (`tests/Unit/PrivateProperty/PpFeatureAttributesTest.php`, `tests/Unit/Syndication/Property24FeatureTagsTest.php`) must be RUN on dev/laragon via `dev-check.ps1`. No migration, no route/perm/nav change. Files: `PrivatePropertyListingMapper.php`, `Property24ListingMapper.php`, audit doc. Still OPEN from the audit (not this pass): PP-B3 datatype live read-back (Family_TV_Room/Entrance_hall/StaffQuarters/Study count-vs-boolean — potential PP106), PP-G2 ScenicView vocabulary, P24 content gaps (zoneType/eyeSpy360/commercial leaseType/unitName/subtype tags). > _Prior:_ 2026-07-04 by **P24 SUBMIT-TIMEOUT HOTFIX — a transient Property24 timeout no longer clobbers a LIVE listing to 'error' → LIVE `main`**. Symptom (Johan): property **1357** (ref **117201765**) showed `P24 Ref: 117201765 — Error  Error: Connection failed: cURL error 28: Operation timed out after 120000ms with 0 bytes received` — a listing that was STILL LIVE on the portal, mislabelled broken; **5 submit timeouts on 2026-07-04** (P24-side slowness — 0 bytes back within the 120s read timeout; today also 16 connect-timeouts on harmless `status_check`). ROOT CAUSE: `Property24SyndicationService::performSubmit()` wrote a permanent `p24_syndication_status='error'` + the raw cURL string into `p24_last_error` on ANY save failure — INCLUDING a transient timeout (no HTTP status). The `isTransientFailure()` classifier already existed and was correctly used by `deactivate/reactivate` (AT-P24 #5) but **never by the submit/update path**. An `error` row additionally (a) lost every UI recovery button (View/Refresh/Deactivate require active|submitted|submitting) and (b) was excluded from `syncAllActivations()` reconcile → **stranded**. FIX (root-cause, mirrors AT-P24 #5): `performSubmit` now branches transient→`handleTransientSubmitFailure()` — **has p24_ref → keep 'active'** (it's still live) + amber "Sync deferred — still live; tap Refresh to retry" note; **no ref → 'pending'** (retryable), never a hard error. Permanent 4xx (validation) → unchanged crimson `error`. UI (`properties/show.blade.php`): sync-state poller no longer shows a FALSE "success" toast when a deferred note is present, and a new amber status line surfaces the note on reload (buttons stay). REMEDIATION: property 1357 verified live via a real `isOnPortal` call (`data:true`) → reset to `active`/enabled, error cleared. TEST: `tests/Feature/Syndication/Property24SubmitTransientFailureTest.php` (2 cases: live-listing timeout stays active / first-submit timeout → pending). ⚠️ the LIVE `/corex` box is `composer install --no-dev` (no phpunit/collision) → this test must be RUN on dev/laragon via `dev-check.ps1`; here it was `php -l`-clean and the transient classification tinker-verified (timeout/503→transient, 422→permanent). Files: `Property24SyndicationService.php`, `resources/views/corex/properties/show.blade.php`, new test. No migration, no new route/perm.

Prior: **AT-135 — WhatsApp `occurred_at` TIMEZONE fix (was 2h-behind UTC → looked like "ingestion stopped at 16:55") + opt-in 419 reload** (Staging merge `02cc51d9`; deployed). Johan's "capture STOPPED at 16:55" was a FALSE alarm — DB had messages through 18:55+ (Elize comm 110 captured, linked, opted_in, 19 ingest POSTs all 200). Root cause = DISPLAY bug: `WaArchiveIngestor::toDate()` used `Carbon::createFromTimestamp()` (UTC); Laravel stores a Carbon's wall-clock AS-IS while `created_at`=`now()` is SAST → `occurred_at` 120min behind; the contact tab/archive ORDER BY + DISPLAY it, so 18:55 showed as 16:55. FIX = `->setTimezone(config('app.timezone'))` in toDate; backfilled 15 staging WA rows `occurred_at += 2h`. RULE: a Carbon written to a datetime column must be app-tz not UTC. "Could not save" on opt-in = CSRF 419 (stale token post re-link; opt-in DID save on the 200) → `decide()` now reloads on 419. Test `WaLidBackfillTargetTest` 6/18. > _Prior:_ 2026-06-26 by **AT-106 — daily self-cleaning P24 location sync (stamp-and-sweep) → LIVE (direct to main)**. Answers "how do we keep provinces/cities/suburbs always correct so a phantom can't recur": `p24:sync-locations` now **stamps `p24_verified_at=now()` on every province/city/suburb P24 returns**, then **soft-deletes anything it did NOT return this run** (verified_at < runStart) — and is **scheduled daily at 11:00** (`routes/console.php`, `withoutOverlapping`; the old monthly entry removed as redundant). This makes the tree self-healing: removed P24 locations (the city-tier staleness AT-105 found — Durban North/785 etc.) get swept automatically; new ones appear. **Safety:** the full walk aborts on ANY fetch error before pruning, AND an **absolute sanity floor** (P24 must return ≥ 5 provinces / 50 cities / 3000 suburbs) skips the sweep on a truncated/auth-broken reply so an API blip can never wipe the tree (deliberately absolute, NOT a ratio-of-current-table — the table is bloated with stale rows the first sweep must clear). Pruned suburbs remediate dependent properties (FK chain nulled + `p24_suburb_mismatch=1`); pruned cities/provinces null the matching property FK. Soft-delete only (#1) → recoverable, and a returned location is revived via `withTrashed()->updateOrCreate`. **Per-agency runs do NOT prune** (`--no-prune` added to `AgencyController` cred-validation syncs + `SyncP24LocationsJob` when agency-scoped) — only the authoritative global daily run sweeps. New `--no-prune` flag on the command. Migration `2026_06_26_140000` adds `p24_verified_at` + soft-deletes to `p24_provinces`/`p24_cities` (suburbs already had them from AT-105) + backfills existing rows. Test `P24LocationSweepTest` (healthy run sweeps only unstamped rows / floor skips on a partial run). **FIRST SWEEP DONE on live** (manual run, observed): swept **197 stale cities + 6,108 suburbs** (6,107 stale + the AT-105 phantom); now 9 provinces / 616 cities / 20,754 suburbs active, **0 active rows left unstamped**, **267/267 syndicating listings kept their `p24_suburb_id`**, **0 properties remediated** (nothing depended on a pruned location). All soft-deleted → recoverable. **Resilience fix (commit `0df9cf9a`):** the first attempt aborted on a single cURL-28 timeout (P24 slow on one cityId) — by design it aborted BEFORE pruning (0 pruned, syndication intact), proving the safety. Every P24 fetch is now wrapped in `fetchRetry` (bounded exponential backoff on transient connection/5xx/429, fail-fast on definitive 4xx, still throws-before-prune if P24 is truly down). Supersedes the AT-105 "AT-106 follow-up" note (reconcile is now obsoleted by the sweep for routine upkeep; keep `p24:reconcile-suburbs` as a manual one-off). The importer page (`/admin/importer/p24-locations`) progress panel now shows a sweep summary on completion ("Swept N stale locations (X cities, Y suburbs) · Z properties remediated", or "Sweep skipped — tree left intact"). Commits: `ad190521` (sweep) + `cd6890c0` (schema) + `0df9cf9a` (retry) + UI line.
>
> _Prior:_ 2026-06-26 by **AT-105 — P24 phantom-suburb existence guard + reconcile → LIVE (direct to main)**. Closes the class behind AT-104's Addington/5997 phantom: `p24_suburbs` rows could carry a `p24_id` P24 never returns, and `AppliesP24Location` only checked the suburb→city→province chain was *internally consistent* — never that the `p24_id` actually exists on P24 (so the phantom passed, saved on prop 5747, P24 bounced it HTTP 400 "SuburbId is invalid"). Fix = one authoritative signal `p24_suburbs.p24_verified_at` ("P24 returned this exact p24_id under this city in the last sync/reconcile"). **(A)** migration adds the column + backfills every existing non-deleted row (= updated_at) so live saves keep working; `SyncP24Locations` now stamps `now()` on every updateOrCreate. **(B) guard:** `AppliesP24Location` rejects any suburb with NULL `p24_verified_at`; `P24LocationController::suburbs()` only offers verified rows (phantoms unselectable + unsaveable on BOTH property paths). **(C) cleanup:** a deterministic migration soft-deletes the proven phantom (matched by p24_id 5997 + name, not local row id) + remediates prop 5747 (FK chain nulled, `p24_suburb_mismatch=1` → agent re-picks; Addington is in P24 *nowhere*); new `php artisan p24:reconcile-suburbs {--apply}` live-diffs every city's P24 suburb list, stamps survivors, soft-deletes stale rows (cities whose fetch FAILS are skipped, never pruned on a network error) + remediates their properties — **dry-run by default**. Note: admin manual-add rows carry `p24_city_id=NULL` (already guard-rejected) and are never stamped verified, so that ingress stays closed without a fragile per-save live call. Test `tests/Feature/Syndication/P24SuburbVerifiedGuardTest.php` (3 paths: verified accepted / phantom rejected / endpoint hides phantom). **DEPLOYED on live** (commits `54afdb48` code + `67ccb1e9` schema snapshot, pushed to main): `migrate` ran A+B on prod (26,819 active rows backfilled verified; phantom 5997 soft-deleted + prop 5747 remediated to NULL/mismatch=1; 0 properties left orphaned); `schema:dump` committed; config/route/view/cache cleared; `queue:restart` + php8.{2,3,4}-fpm reloaded (live `/corex` worker respawned on fresh code). Guard verified on live (verified suburb accepted, unverified rejected). phpunit is a dev-dep absent on the box — run `P24SuburbVerifiedGuardTest` via the Windows dev-check. **Reconcile dry-run finding (NOT applied):** the suburb universe under live P24 cities is CLEAN (0 prunes across 86 sampled cities; the one phantom was already migration-purged), so `--apply` would change ~nothing now. BUT it exposed a **city-tier staleness**: ~most local `p24_cities` rows return P24 `400 "City with Id X does not exist"` (e.g. Durban North/785, Ezakheni/170) — stale ids P24 removed that `updateOrCreate` never prunes. The reconcile safely SKIPS them (never prunes a suburb on a city-fetch failure). **Recommended follow-up (AT-106):** extend reconcile to the city tier (soft-delete cities P24 no longer returns via getCities) and/or re-run `p24:sync-locations`, THEN a full `p24:reconcile-suburbs --apply`. New migrations: `2026_06_26_120000` (column) + `2026_06_26_120001` (phantom purge).

> _Prior:_ 2026-06-26 by **AT-104 — P24 suburb resolution hotfix → LIVE (direct to main, no staging)**. Collision suburb names were syndicating to the wrong P24 city — South Coast "Glenmore" (Port Edward, p24_id 10790) listings showed as "Durban" (10787). Root cause in `Property24ListingMapper::resolveSuburbId()`: tier 1 checked `pp_suburb_id` (a Private Property column NULL on every CoreX property → branch never fired), then fell through to `P24Suburb::lookup()->first()` — a bare name match, no city filter — picking whichever same-named row sorted first. Fix: trust the stored chain-verified `p24_suburb_id` FK first (fixes 100% of the 265 enabled listings); else name match **disambiguated by city/province**, returned only on a UNIQUE match; else `null` → `validate()` skips + flags ("Suburb unmapped — manual P24 suburb mapping required"); never a guessed fallback. Removed the name-only `/suburbs/find` auto-resolve + bare fuzzy fallback (could re-introduce the bug; zero enabled props relied on them; `p24:sync-locations` keeps `p24_suburbs` complete). Province text now normalises both sides (P24 stores "KwaZulu Natal", CoreX holds "KwaZulu-Natal"/"KZN"). Commit `0709f69d` on main; queue:restart + `corex-worker-live` restarted + booted clean (P24 sync 222/0 errors post-restart). **Verified on LIVE:** re-synced sample props 5747/5762/5831 → `request_payload.suburbId` now **10790** (was 10787), HTTP 200. New `tests/Feature/Syndication/Property24SuburbResolutionTest.php` (6 paths) committed — phpunit is a dev-dep absent on the live box, so verification was via tinker against the live DB. **⚠️ BACKFILL AWAITING JOHAN'S GO (do NOT auto-run):** 8 live listings still hold the old wrong suburbId — props **2020, 3894, 5860, 5862, 5891** (Glenmore 10787→10790), **2821** (Bulwer, Durban 14226→5969), **3307** (Rocklands, Port Edward 18357→18249), **5900** (Melville, Port Shepstone 4145→10881). 0 listings now resolve to null (nothing previously-syndicating gets skipped). ## 1. Identity & Stack

**Who:** Johan Reichel (CEO, HFC). Andre Roets (full-stack dev). Two-person team building CoreX OS — real estate operating system. HFC (Home Finders Coastal) is the first live agency. Long-term vision: SA's leading real estate OS, replacing PropCon / Sage / Property24 layers across the industry.

**Stack:** Laravel 12 / Blade / Alpine.js. MySQL prod (`hfc_corex`, `hfc_staging`). SQLite local. Vite. Ubuntu on Hetzner `91.99.130.85`. Code at `/corex` (live) and `/corex-staging`. Python AI service `/opt/hf-ai/app.py` port 3100 (not in git).

**Domain:** `corex.hfcoastal.co.za` live. Staging on port 8084.

**Branches:** `main` (live), `Staging`, `HFC2402` (Johan dev), `andre` (Andre dev), feature branches off Staging. Discipline: HFC2402 + andre → Staging → staging server → main → live. Hotfix exception: direct to main, then back-sync to Staging.

**VS Code Claude** is the coding agent. Johan pastes prompts, it executes. Specs in `.ai/specs/`, read at start of every prompt.

## 1.5 Operating Principle (read this first, every chat)

CoreX is the best real estate operating system that will ever exist. This is the decision filter for every prompt, every architectural choice, every "should we ship this now" call.

- Best-in-class or rebuild — if competitors do something better, we build ours better
- No shortcuts ever — later does not exist; build it right the first time
- Integration is the moat — every feature seamlessly connects to every other
- Built for agents, not screens — we absorb complexity so they don't have to
- AI enhances, never replaces human judgement
- Constraint is fuel — build best with what we have, never use lack of resources as an excuse

Decision test before any commit: **does this make CoreX the best, or does it make CoreX merely working?** If the answer is "working", redesign.

"Good enough for now" is never the answer. "We'll fix it later" is never the answer.

See CLAUDE.md "CoreX Operating Principle" section for the full version.

## 2. Working Rules

- **Investigate before fixing.** Every issue: (1) audit, (2) Johan approves fix approach, (3) only then fix prompt. Never guess root causes.
- **One concern per prompt.** Two only if tightly related and same file.
- **Surgical changes.** No refactoring beyond scope.
- **Every prompt opens:** read CLAUDE.md, .ai/STANDARDS.md, relevant spec, and this file.
- **Every prompt closes:** php -l, php artisan view:clear, scripts/dev-check.ps1 if structural change, Tinker verification, **update this CHAT_STARTER.md**.
- **No hard deletes.** SoftDeletes only.
- **PPRA not EAAB. POPIA consent rules apply.**
- **Bug report = code is wrong.** Never blame caching or user error.

## 4. Recent decisions log (last 15, newest top)

- **2026-07-07** — **AT-57 follow-up: wizard is now FULLY INLINE — no step deep-links out to settings** (Johan feedback: "no open new tab, all settings should sit on this onboarding setup"). Removed every "Open … editor" link. Added two rendering modes to the wizard beyond the data-driven scalar controls: (1) **inline partials** rendered inside the wizard's own `<form>` for rich forms — commission (splits/caps/fees/mentor + 7-tier revenue-share table), notifications (reminder + channel toggles), compliance (whistleblow routing) — whose fields carry the exact input names the canonical saver expects, so they still post through the wizard to the same `SettingsController`/`CommissionSettingsController` method (zero drift preserved); (2) **aux collection editors** (`config.aux_partial`) rendered OUTSIDE the main form (so add/remove sub-forms aren't nested) for list settings — property types/statuses/mandate/condition + contact sources — posting to new wizard sub-routes `corex.agency-setup.collection.add|remove` that delegate to the canonical `storePropertySettingItem`/`destroyPropertySettingItem`/`ContactSourceController` CRUD. GOTCHA: contact **types** are system-locked (`ContactTypeController::store()` returns `locked()`) and contact tags need a parent type — so types render read-only and only sources are inline-addable. Regression guard `test_no_step_deep_links_out_of_the_wizard` iterates all 9 steps. 25/25 tests (was 20). Spec §3.3a.
- **2026-07-07** — **AT-57 AGENCY ONBOARDING SETUP WIZARD built (branch, HOLD).** Decision: the emailed setup link is gated by the Admin's **real CoreX login** (not a throwaway password) because the wizard writes **live** agency data — so every save runs under normal `auth` + `agency.required` + per-section permission, correctly scoped/audited. Decision: the wizard **must not** own a parallel settings system — each step **invokes the exact `SettingsController` save method** the settings page uses (`app(SettingsController::class)->method($request)`), so the two can never drift; a saver's permission-403 is absorbed (control skipped), a ValidationException bubbles to re-render the step. Decision: trigger via new **`App\Events\AgencyCreated`** domain event (NOT an ad-hoc hook; added to the events catalogue), fired post-commit from `AgencyController@store` **only when `$adminPayload` exists** so demo agencies get nothing. Decision: distinct route prefix `/agency-setup/{token}` (P24 already owns `onboarding/{token}` as a single-segment wildcard — would shadow). Decision: a **completed** setup stays re-openable in the browser (the one deliberate divergence from P24's 410-on-complete) since it's the Admin's own setup. Complex collection editors (commission tiers, property/contact type lists, compliance officer appointments) are honestly **deep-linked** to their existing full editors rather than rebuilt in-wizard. GOTCHA: fresh test DB has no `role_permissions` → PermissionService "allow-all" fallback, so a plain admin passes every gate in tests without seeding. 17/17 tests green. Spec `.ai/specs/agency-onboarding-setup.md`. **Deploy still owed** (dev env has no host SSH): migrate + `corex:sync-permissions --merge-defaults` on the target.
- **2026-07-07** — **MIC "THIS WEEK" TILE BUTTONS FIXED → LIVE (main) + Staging.** Andre reported the Work-tab hero buttons (Pitch now / View pocket / See new) don't work. CAUSE 1 (the "do nothing"): tiles cached by `WarmThisWeekTilesJob` @02:30 in a queue context (no request host) → `route()` baked absolute `https://corexos.co.za`; `session.domain=NULL` = host-only cookies → agents on canonical `corex.hfcoastal.co.za` clicked → cross-domain nav → no session → login bounce. FIX: `ThisWeekTileBuilder` emits RELATIVE `action_url`s (`route(...,[],false)`) — works on any domain, and the nightly job can never bake a cross-domain host again. CAUSE 2 (mismatch/empty): tile counts came from different queries than their links — matches 4592 (raw match rows) vs `pitch_now_high` 829; new 7 (`tracked_properties` since Friday) vs `new_today` 0 → "See new" landed on an EMPTY list; pocket 6 (demand) vs 1 (supply). FIX: preset logic extracted to `App\Services\Prospecting\ProspectingActionPresetService` (single source of truth); `MarketIntelligenceController::applyActionPreset` delegates to it; the tile builder counts THROUGH it, mirroring work()'s `groupBy(property_group_id ?? 'single_'.id)` so the count == the rows you land on; pocket headlines supply (demand as context); any tile with an empty destination is suppressed. Live-verified for Andre: matches 829==829, pocket 1==1, new-tile correctly hidden. Cleared all `tiles:user:%` cache rows so every agent gets fresh relative-URL tiles. Test `ThisWeekTileConsistencyTest` (grouping-collapse + relative-URL). MIC spec addendum. GOTCHA: `route()` in a queue/CLI context falls back to APP_URL's host — never cache absolute app URLs; build relative.

- **2026-07-07** — **CALENDAR BLACKOUT ROOT-FIXED → LIVE (main) + Staging.** Kym + all 22 HFC agents had genuinely-empty calendars (events all present in DB). ROOT CAUSE (identified): the **AT-197 Part A "turn-off"** — a developer/agent session deliberately turned OFF all 49 classes for HFC via agency-1 override rows (`is_active=false`, faithful global copies), a documented "setup-session" op with a restoration baseline (`.ai/audits/2026-07-06-event-classes-snapshot.md`). The 18:19-create / 05:10-update stamps are its two passes (first 500'd on a JSON-cast bug, re-run). CRITICAL: AT-197's impact statement ASSUMED inactive = "materialised but inert / agents keep working normally" — but the real code returned NULL and dropped the events. The fix makes reality match that assumption. `CalendarThresholdResolver::resolveForEvent()` returned NULL for an inactive class; `CalendarController::applyFilters()` + `CalendarTileService` DROP every null-colour event → whole book vanished. Only HFC because agency 1 is the ONLY agency with agency-specific override rows, and `forAgencyAndClass()` returns an agency row even when inactive → the dead overrides shadowed the active globals. FIX (fix-the-class): inactive/missing class config resolves to `'neutral'` (visible, no urgency), NEVER null — a class-config state must never ERASE an existing event; deactivating stops new-event generation+RAG+notifications only. `'neutral'` was already a valid resolved colour (beyond-green case) so zero downstream change; owners always pass `canSee` via the creator rule. REJECTED a blanket active-global fallback in `forAgencyAndClass` (would delete per-agency deactivation entirely). DATA: reactivated the 48 rows to restore RAG immediately, then reset them to global via `resetEventClass` semantics (47/48 byte-identical copies of globals = accidental shadow; `manual` differed only in notifications; ALL backed up to storage first — model has NO SoftDeletes, so hard-delete of the thin override layer is the sanctioned "reset to global"). Test `InactiveClassStillRendersTest` (active→RAG, inactive→neutral, incident-shape override→neutral, resolve() null only when dateless). Spec §17. GOTCHA: resolver memoizes `forAgencyAndClass` in-process → a CLI/tinker `is_active` change needs `flushResolveCache()` + an fpm reload or live workers serve stale null.

- **2026-07-07** — **CALENDAR VIEW-SAVE TRAP FIXED → LIVE (main) + Staging.** Kym Pollard reported "calendar empty / most entries gone" — a FALSE alarm on data: all 431 of her events were present; her `default_view` had silently flipped to `day` so she landed on a single day (~4 entries). ROOT CAUSE: every event-click routes to `?view=day` (deep-link), and §16.4's "Save default" read `body.view = $currentView` (server-rendered) — so an agent who clicked an event then saved their tile arrangement silently promoted Day to their default view. **5 of 6 agents** (Kym, Shalan + Shawn Du Bois, Dru De Bruyn, Gerda Baard) were locked into Day within 2 days of the cockpit shipping. REMEDIATION: reset those 5 `default_view`→`month` (live DB). FIX (Johan ruling "keep, but only user-chosen view"): `save()` now promotes `view`/`scroll_mode` ONLY when present in the TRANSIENT (`window.CoreXCal.get()`) — which is written solely by the view switcher / Stream·Pages toggle (deliberate choice); event-click/deep-link views never touch the transient → omitted from the POST → `saveCockpit`'s `array_key_exists && !==null` guard leaves the saved default untouched. Same fix on `scroll_mode` (fix the class). Test `CalendarExplicitSaveTest::test_save_without_view_leaves_the_existing_default_view_untouched`. Spec §16.9. GOTCHA: the transient key IS the deliberate-choice signal — no new state needed.

- **2026-07-06** — **AT-177 WS6 cutover machinery + compensator retirement → Staging `29395931` (cc2, HELD from live).** KEY DECISIONS: the cutover is a per-template `compiled_serving` flag (agency-blind, template-level, REVERSIBLE) — `SigningController::show()` gets an ADDITIVE compiled-serving branch at the top of the web-template path, the legacy body wrapped UNTOUCHED in `else` (minimal diff = safest for the P0 signing file + satisfies the pipeline gate with a SigningView test diff). DUAL-PATH coexistence is the design: non-cutover templates serve byte-for-byte as before (proven by regressing template-111 through the real /sign route). The compiled path calls ZERO of the 7 §9 compensators (verified) — "retirement" = structural absence for compiled templates; the compensator CODE is RETAINED until no template serves legacy (actual deletion = a later gated commit, per §9's standing rule). HELD the in-situ staging-HOST flip because cc3 is deploying live/staging hotfixes to the shared host — a signing-runtime deploy mid-storm risks Johan's live-QA; delivered the runbook instead. GOTCHA: `git commit -m` with backticks/`$` in the message → bash command-substitutes them → tokens vanish; use `git commit -F <file>`. [[at177-esign-compiler-ws6]]

- **2026-07-04** — **AT-164 — To-dos tile "no activity in -0.605…days" FIXED (day-diff bug-class) → Staging `fa7d91d3`, DEPLOYED `/corex-staging`.** Root cause = Carbon 3 `diffInDays()` returns a SIGNED FLOAT; `now()->diffInDays($past)` is negative+fractional. Raw → broke the to-do title; `(int)`-cast → truncated toward zero + went negative, silently corrupting day counters AND threshold comparisons (`PropertyHealthCalculator`'s `$daysSince > 30` never true for a negative → idle property scored healthy). Fixed the CLASS: NEW `App\Support\HumanDiff` (`daysBetween()` absolute whole calendar days, never neg/fractional; `days()` → "today"/"1 day"/"13 days"), routed every elapsed-diff text/number path through it (AutoEventService title+critical flag, PropertyHealthCalculator labels+penalties, CommandCentreService days_overdue/on_market/waiting/buyer-idle). Left `diffForHumans()` bodies (Carbon-correct) + cockpit week-row geometry (cc3's surface) untouched — tile CONTENT/service only. - **2026-06-30** — **AT-130 — ONE canonical OtpService (build-once OTP engine), ClientAuth migrated onto it (no second engine).** Preceded by the OTP sweep (`.ai/audits/2026-06-30-at130-otp-engine-sweep.md`): the only real OTP was ClientAuth's client-portal login (`ClientOtp` + `issueOtp/verifyOtp`); Andre's "mobile OTP" = that same one, mobile-consumed via `/api/v1/client-auth/otp/*`; `TvAccessCode` is a pairing code, not an OTP; "OTP" in esign = "Offer To Purchase". Field clear → build. **Engine** `App\Services\Otp\OtpService`: generate 6-digit **hashed at rest**; deliver via the **sender-only** `otp` mailer to **the consumer's destination** (never a fixed mailbox → break-glass-to-requester's-own-email satisfiable WITHOUT touching the mailer); validate latest unused/unexpired/matching-purpose, **single-use**, attempts++ on miss; **throttle** (resend cooldown + hourly cap) per (bucket,destination); **audit** every issue+verify to a **CONSUMER-PROVIDED sink** — engine hard-codes NO sink and NO role/capability check (capability = consumer's concern). Defaults `config/otp.php` carried over verbatim from clientauth (6/10min/5/60s/5-per-hr), overridable per call. **Store**: generalised `client_otps` **IN PLACE** (additive, live-safe, NO rename — seeder/test/relation reference the name) — +`subject_type/subject_id` (generic polymorphic subject), `destination`, `channel`; backfill `destination=email`; relax legacy `email`→NULL. `App\Models\Otp` = canonical model (table `client_otps`); `ClientOtp` now a BC subclass (keeps `ClientUser->otps()` + fixtures); `Otp::creating` mirrors `email→destination` for BC. **ClientAuth migrated, behaviour identical**: `issueOtp/verifyOtp` delegate to OtpService (destination=client email, subject=ClientUser, `ClientAuthOtpMail` preserved, fake-`@corexclient.co.za` skip preserved, legacy `client_user_id`+`email` still populated, `ClientAccessLog otp_sent` sink preserved); controller issuance throttle now `OtpService->throttle('client_login', email)` (bucket shared across activation+recovery = prior per-email keying). **Verify** (Tinker rolled-back tx + endpoint, NO dev-check): php -l clean; migrate up/down/up clean; schema snapshot regenerated; **Tinker 28/28 PASS** (hash-at-rest, single-use, attempt-cap, expiry, arbitrary-destination delivery, client-login parity, fake-domain skip, throttle, audit-routes-to-consumer-sink/engine-writes-nothing-to-ClientAccessLog); **`ClientAuthFlowTest` OTP 3/3** (HTTP `/otp/send`+`/otp/verify`). **RESERVED AT-132 Wave 2 (noted, NOT built):** `comms_break_glass` consumer (capability `communications.grant_access`, destination=requester's own verified email, success=thread-scoped session grant, sink=`comms_access_audit_log`; ⚠️ before wiring, `CommsAccessAuditLog::EVENT_TYPES` must gain `otp_issued`+`otp_unlock` or `record()` throws). `TvAccessCode` left alone. - **2026-06-24** — **AT-94 FICA model fix: FICA is a SELLER-CONTACT gate, not a property document (removes duplication + closes two holes).** Johan-approved after an investigation confirmed FICA was being gated as a property-Drive doc type AND (via an OR-bridge) the contact's `fica_submissions` — a duplicate, weaker path. Two holes found: (1) a scanned "FICA.pdf" on the property Drive satisfied the gate with NO seller actually FICA-approved (instant-unlock doctrine, no status check); (2) there was NO explicit "property must have a linked seller" gate, so a property with zero contacts could go live if the 3 docs sat on the property Drive. FIX: the `fica` required-type is now satisfied ONLY by `checkSellersFicaSubmissions` — ≥1 linked seller/owner/landlord/lessor AND **every** one `fica_submissions.status='approved'`; Drive FICA docs are ignored for the gate. `evaluateRequiredTypes()` special-cases the fica slug (config `fica_slug`) → contact gate; mandate/disclosure stay property-Drive docs. FICA stays in the agency-configurable required list (default on — Johan chose agency-configurable over always-on; an agency can untick it). Checklist: FICA renders as a *seller-contact status row* linking to `compliance.fica.create?contact_id=…` (or "Link a seller" when none), NOT a property upload. - **2026-06-21** — **AT-75: MIC reads the canonical match truth; "Buyer matched" is two threshold-anchored honest units.** DECISIONS: (1) The prospecting cache (`prospecting_buyer_matches`) is scored by the SHARED canonical engine `MatchingService::score` (only criteria the buyer specified contribute — no Engine-B no-signal phantom defaults that made a near-empty wishlist score ~85 on every listing). Core Matches identical); prospecting passes `mic_price_band_pct` (±10% default). (3) `score()` now skips the category/property_type component when the PROPERTY side is null — CoreX "incomplete listings shouldn't be penalised" (prospecting listings carry no category; a category-specifying buyer was wrongly dragged to 62 on every listing). A present-but-different value still scores 0 (real mismatch). (4) The "Buyer matched" KPI is now TWO threshold-anchored units (agency `mic_match_threshold`, default 75%): `buyers_matched` = distinct countable buyers with a real match ≥ threshold (this is the pipeline-reconciling number — only countable buyers are ever cached), `properties_matched` = distinct canvass listings ≥ threshold; tile clickable → worklist filtered to the band. - **2026-06-21** — **AT-74 HOTFIX: two staging bugs from Build 4.** (1) Blade does not parse an `@if` directive glued to a preceding word character (`demand@if(...)`) but DOES parse the trailing `@endif` → a stray endif 500'd the whole presentation page. LESSON: never glue a Blade `@directive` to a preceding word; inline conditionals in text should use an echo ternary `{{ cond ? a : b }}`, not `@if…@endif`. Also: `php artisan view:cache` SWALLOWS blade parse errors (exits 0) — to truly lint a blade, compile via `Blade::compileString` and `php -l` the output (raw @if/@endif counts can balance while the structure is broken, because @unless/@isset/@auth/@can/@error also emit if/endif). (2) MIC "Buyer matched" = 0 was NOT cache-lag and NOT a wrong-table read — the recompute writes the right table (`prospecting_buyer_matches`) but a broad wishlist matching thousands of canvass listings made `recomputeProspectingMatchesForBuyer` build a single `upsert()` exceeding MySQL's 65,535-placeholder limit (SQLSTATE 1390); the throw was swallowed by `RegenerateBuyerMatchesJob`'s per-contact try/catch, leaving the table empty. FIX (fix-the-class): `chunkedUpsert()` wraps all 3 Engine B match-cache upserts at 500 rows/statement. Staging: recompute → 14,996 matches, MIC 0→7,407. Test `ProspectingMatchChunkedUpsertTest` (600 matches across 2 chunks). NB the 7,407 reflects 2 very broad test wishlists under the lenient no-signal scoring (consistent with Core Matches/Intelligence) — scoring-tuning, not a bug. Files: `presentations/show.blade.php`, `PropertyMatchScoringService` (chunkedUpsert + 3 call sites), test.

- **2026-06-21** — **AT-72: the Buyer Pipeline is the spine — a countable wishlist must AUTO-LAND a buyer on it.** DECISION: creating a countable wishlist (ContactMatch, AT-71 `isCountable()`) is itself enough to make a contact an active buyer — it should not require a separate activity first. `ContactMatchObserver::created()` (insert-only, gated on `isCountable()`, failure-wrapped) calls the new `BuyerStateService::landOnPipeline()`, which sets `is_buyer=true` + stamps `buyer_pipeline_entered_at`, then transitions `buyer_state='new'` (audited in `buyer_state_transitions`, reason `wishlist_created`) ONLY when the buyer has no state yet — an existing Warm/Cold/Lost buyer is NEVER reset by adding another wishlist, and multiple wishlists land the buyer exactly once (idempotent). An empty/uncountable wishlist does NOT land anyone (no pipeline inflation — consistent with the AT-71 countable gate). ROOT-CAUSE CLASS FIX (BUILD_STANDARD §6): `transitionTo` never set `agency_id` on `BuyerStateTransition`, which is NOT-NULL (2026_05_23_030800) with no DB default — every transition insert 1364-failed on a multi-agency DB (the dev/staging shape), a latent bug that also silently broke `markActivity` + the daily recompute cron; it was masked only because single-agency DBs auto-stamp via BelongsToAgency. Now set explicitly from `$contact->agency_id` (single insert site, grep-confirmed). Schema: extended `buyer_state_transitions.reason` enum with `wishlist_created` + `auto_landed` via raw `ALTER` migration `2026_06_21_041100` (down() re-narrows after normalising rows) + schema snapshot re-dumped. Two commits. **`c51c0607` (identity):** `CompLabel::build()` Fix A inverts priority for sectional rows — when `scheme_name` AND a section token are both present it returns "Unit {section}, {scheme}" (Unit-first, matching `Property::buildDisplayAddress()`), ahead of the street address (the street on a sectional row is the scheme's shared, non-unique street). DECISION: gate the override on BOTH columns filled (mirrors `AnalysisDataService.php:163`) rather than the prompt's literal "scheme OR section" — scheme-only/section-only rows keep the existing address-first chain so nothing regresses. `CmaInfoPropertyValuationParser` Fix B threads `$subject['scheme_name']` into `extractCmaCompRows()` and attributes the scheme-less + street-less in-scheme units to the subject scheme (mirrors `CmaInfoSectionalTitleSalesParser:299`); out-of-scheme comps set both scheme+address via the per-row lookback and so skip the fallback. Audited on hfc_staging (pres 98 / report 162 / PUMULA): 45 comps = 23 priority-bug (had complex, showed street) + 22 capture-bug (lost complex) + 0 correct → after the batch + re-import all render complex-first. Tests: CompLabelTest (14), new CmaInfoPropertyValuationSchemeBackfillTest (3), ReviewCompTableAddressTest assertion bump. **`57a98460` (PDF):** `.avoid-break` group around the holding-cost tiles + callout; comp-table `<thead>` → `display:table-header-group` + rows `page-break-inside:avoid`; evidence badges → "Recent sale" / "Area average". NO backfill tooling — agency re-imports CMAs before each presentation, so re-import report 162 + re-generate pres 98 materialises the corrected labels. PARKED: pre-existing `ReviewCompTableAddressTest` route-302 (baseline, not this batch).
- **2026-06-18** — **GPS-BORROW-FIX: subject pin no longer borrows a sibling property's GPS** (same branch `feat-ss-presentation-complex-identity`; **committed locally, then pushed + deployed to `/corex-staging` via the SS-COMPLEX-IDENTITY batch FF**). Property 771 (Duke Road, Margate) rendered ~1.2 km off and showed "0 comps within 1km". ROOT CAUSE: `AddressResolverService::resolveFromMarketReports` (the market-report borrow branch) OR-ed its address-needle match with a bare `source_suburb = ?` clause, so when a suburb was known EVERY same-suburb report matched and `orderByDesc('id')` returned a sibling's `subject_latitude/longitude` — 771 inherited Acacia Road's pin (`-30.8468120, 30.3764720`, market_reports 93/94) and it was cached as confidence `exact` (geocoding_cache row 6147 `duke road margate`), so it re-served forever. THREE-PART FIX: **(i)** an address-needle match is now REQUIRED (`if (empty($needles)) return null` — suburb alone never borrows); the suburb clause becomes an optional CONFIRM (`source_suburb = ? OR NULL/''`) that only NARROWS a needle match so a same-street-name report in a different suburb can't be borrowed. **(ii)** `resolve()` gains a `bypassCache` param — a re-resolve skips the cache READ but still write-throughs via `cacheAndReturn` (updateOrCreate), so a previously-poisoned entry is OVERWRITTEN instead of re-served. **(iii)** `PropertyGeoBackfillService::backfillProperty` now resolves when `pinIsSuspect()` (suburb-centroid/unresolved/low-confidence) not just on null/force, passes `bypassCache: $latLngBefore` on re-resolves, and a new `confidenceRank()` guard (exact 5 > street 4 > suburb 3 > town 2 > unknown 1 > failed 0) means a re-resolve NEVER downgrades a good pin — replacing the old "overwrite only if null" which was itself a bug-class making any wrong coord permanent. `PresentationGeneratorService` subject-geocode trigger extended to `|| pinIsSuspect()`. **Tests:** 4 green in `tests/Feature/Geo/SubjectGpsBorrowFixTest.php` (suburb-never-borrows / address-match-beats-higher-id-sibling / suspect-self-heals-bypassing-poisoned-cache-and-upgrades / guard-never-downgrades). Two needed fixture fixes only — `Property::create` was missing `agent_id` (→ no-default) then `branch_id` (PropertyObserver fell back to non-existent id 1 → FK violation); setUp now creates a real Branch + assigns the agent's `branch_id`; the runtime logic was never the failure. **VERIFIED on hfc_staging** (ran the fixed dev code against the staging DB, `force: true`): property 771 `-30.8468120/30.3764720` (Acacia) → **`-30.8578220/30.3742930` (Duke Road truth, from market_report 162)**, NOT Acacia; poisoned geocoding_cache row 6147 overwritten via write-through. **FOLLOW-ON:** (a) the `/corex-staging` checkout is on branch `Staging` and does NOT carry the fix — it must be deployed before the live property page pin/comps reflect the correction; (b) 6 `storage/tmp_*.php` scratch files (dev: marketanchor_audit/pumula_rows/pumula_sweep; staging: complabel_audit/marketanchor_audit/pumula_audit_partB) await manual deletion — `rm` is permission-blocked in this session. Files: `AddressResolverService`, `PropertyGeoBackfillService`, `PresentationGeneratorService`, new `SubjectGpsBorrowFixTest`.

- **2026-06-16** — **PRES-CMA-REALFIX: recommended valuation band = indicated value ± asymmetric % (10% below / 13% above)** (branch `PRES-CMA-REALFIX`, off Staging; **not merged — held for Johan's walkthrough**). **Root problem:** §5/§6 band sourced lower/upper from the raw comp-pool P25/P75. For clean same-type pools that is ~±6%, but type-contaminated pools blew out to ±20%+ — a band wide enough to lose the seller message. **Fix:** `AnalysisDataService::compileCmaValuation` now derives `lower = middle×(1−lower%/100)`, `upper = middle×(1+upper%/100)` from the evaluated value (the comp-median MIDDLE), with the agent's condition % applied EXACTLY ONCE to the middle before the band is derived (no-op today — condition data is 0% populated; verified). Raw P25/median/P75 stay in `pool_stats` for the "Why This Range?" evidence rows only. Verdict anchored to the middle: `is_overpriced = asking > upper`; §6 card colour danger>upper / warning>middle / success, **green impossible above upper**. Live recompile (`PresentationPdfService:582`) means it shows on regenerate with no frozen override; null band (no comps, e.g. PRES 41) suppresses the card (no false green). **The number — asymmetric 10/13, not the 7/7 placeholder:** reverse-engineered CMA's OWN stated low/middle/high across **105 evidenced imported reports** (`market_data_points.cma_value_lower/middle/upper`): median lower gap 11.5% / upper 13.6% (mean 13/16; skewed wider above, ratio 1.25), tightening to ~10%/13% on ≥8-comp reports; **no price-scaling** (the two populated price buckets <R1M and R1–3M are near-identical), so one % across all prices. New agency settings `cma_band_lower_pct`/`cma_band_upper_pct` (decimal, **default 10.00 / 13.00**; separate from the percentile `range_lower/upper_pct` which are p25/p75 and were NOT touched), surfaced agency→`CmaComputeService.pool_stats`→band; `CompPoolBuilder::DEF_BAND_*` fallback matches. Two migrations (`140000` add cols 7/7, `160000` alter default→10/13 + backfill 2 agencies off the 7 default). **Settings → Presentations** got two labelled inputs ("Valuation band — below/above middle (%)", helper "CMA market norm ≈ 10% below, 13% above", 0–40), reachable via Settings sidebar (`corex-sidebar.blade.php:1378`, `permission:access_settings`). Condition % stays editable at Settings → Presentations → "Condition Levels" (`adjustment_pct`) — unchanged. **Verified on real staging data:** PRES 65 band 1,116k–1,284k → 1,080k–1,356k (middle 1,200k unchanged, OVERPRICED held); PRES 5 1,204k–1,386k → 1,166k–1,463k (middle 1,295k, OVERPRICED); setting-flow proof (agency 5/20 → mid×0.95/×1.20 live). `SellerVoiceAnchorTest` extended to pin the asymmetric band (5 passed, 26 assertions; single file per rule #13 — full suite NOT run). schema:dump regenerated. - **2026-06-15** — **AT-43: email completion — Sent special-use, ingestion filter, contact comms tab** (branch `AT-43-email-completion-sent-filter-contact-tab`, off Staging; **not yet merged**). **Fix 1 (outbound capture):** `ImapMailboxPoller` resolved Sent by webklex `getFolderByName()` (leaf name) → on a mailbox with 3 "Sent" folders it grabbed an empty homonym and never read the real `INBOX.Sent` (551 msgs). - **2026-06-15** — **AT-36 Communication Archive — Pending Triage (Phase A) closed out** (off AT-34). The spine's pending-grace buffer now has a staff workflow + BM audit surface, no AI. - **2026-06-12** — **AT-22 item 2 LIVE LEAK fixed at the root — competitor branding now blocked by IMAGE CONTENT, not just URL.** PRES 87 / v175 leaked the RE/MAX "Coast and Country" logo as the "12 Bairn Street" competitor card (PP-T5391969, prospecting_listings #1566). Root cause: `ListingImageValidator` matched brand only on URL/filename SUBSTRINGS, but the card was a competitor logo uploaded as the PrivateProperty listing's primary photo — served from a neutral CDN URL (`images.pp.co.za/listing/…`), stored under a system filename (`pp_PP-T5391969.jpg`), with `thumbnail_source_url` NULL. The brand lived only in the PIXELS, so every substring check passed. Compounding bug: the render gate's `isGenuinePhoto($source_url ?: $thumbPath)` fell back to the neutral stored PATH when the URL was null — a no-op that re-validated nothing. Fix: added an IMAGE-CONTENT layer to `ListingImageValidator` — `inspectImageBytes()/inspectImageFile()` run tesseract OCR for competitor brand-text (`brand:remax` …) + a flat-graphic colour signal (uniq-colours ≤64 AND luminance-entropy <4.0; real PP photos measured 195–283 / 7.25–7.50, a flat brand card 26 / 1.96 — huge margin, near-zero false-positive). Detection runs ONCE at ingress (`DownloadListingThumbnail`, on full-res bytes) and persists to new column `prospecting_listings.thumbnail_blocked_reason`; render gate (`CompetitorStockMatchService::scoreAndMapRow`) + the `corex.market.thumbnail` route both honour it (blocked → "No photo" placeholder / 404). Removed the meaningless `?:` path-fallback. New backfill command `prospecting:rescan-thumbnail-brands` (--only/--dry-run/--rescan) re-inspects historic stored thumbnails — **this is the live remediation: run it on prod to block the existing PP-T5391969 file.** Verified end-to-end against #1566: pre-fix gate `genuine=true` (LEAK) → post-fix `brand:remax` → placeholder + 404. Conservative on every tooling gap (undecodable bytes / missing tesseract → genuine; flat-graphic signal + URL layer still apply). LIVE NOTE: install `tesseract-ocr` on the prod host for brand-TEXT coverage; the flat-graphic signal works without it. Migration added → schema snapshot re-dumped. New tests: `tests/Feature/Prospecting/ListingImageContentValidatorTest.php` (6). Existing `CompetitorBrandingStripTest` (4) traced compatible. Files: `ListingImageValidator`, `DownloadListingThumbnail`, `CompetitorStockMatchService`, `MarketIntelligenceController::thumbnail`, `RescanThumbnailBrands` cmd, `ProspectingListing` model, migration.
- **2026-06-10** — **Push-notification storm fixed at the root (server-side).** A user's handset was bricked by a repeated FCM push. Root cause: two paths (`NotificationDispatcher::sendPush` + the `PushNewPortalLeadToMobile` listener) called the FCM transport directly with **zero guards** — the portal-lead listener fanned out to every device of every agency user on every `NewPortalLeadReceived` event, and the 5-minute P24 poller could re-fire that event for the same lead; duplicate device-token rows multiplied each event into several buzzes. Named culprit: **a fan-out resolving the same device token multiple times + no idempotency/cooldown/bounded-retry**. NOT an observer save-back loop, NOT infinite retry. Fix: one guarded funnel `PushNotificationService` (token dedup → idempotency per (key,device) via `Cache::add` → hard per-device per-minute rate cap → bounded retry+backoff → stale-token prune → per-user/min metrics). `FcmService` reduced to a single-attempt `PushTransport` adapter; `NullPushTransport` is the no-creds fallback bound in `AppServiceProvider`. Idempotency keys are stable per logical event (pillar: `user|event|subject|hourBucket`; portal lead: `portal_lead:{id}`). `DeviceTokenController::store` hardened: one active row per physical device (supersede same token under a new user), revive soft-deleted rows via `withTrashed` (fixes a latent unique-index 500), fully idempotent. `config/push.php` tunables. 13 tests (idempotency, distinct-events, token-dedup, rate cap, retry-cap, retry-then-succeed-once, dead-token-prune, no-op transport, portal-lead storm, device-token registration). Spec `.ai/specs/push-notifications.md`. No migration → no schema re-dump. dev-check clean; full-suite parity confirmed (pre-existing RecipientLoop env failures unchanged).
- **2026-06-06** — **Soft Deletes Register shipped (Admin → Soft Deletes).** One screen surfacing every soft-deleted record across all ~221 `SoftDeletes` models so an admin can restore them. Design (Andre's calls): **restore-only** — no purge/force-delete control anywhere in the UI, fully honouring no-hard-deletes #1 (permanent purge stays console-only via `db:purge-soft-deleted`); cover **all** soft-deletable models via reflection auto-discovery; sits under Admin, gated by new Role-Manager-grantable permission `access_soft_deletes`; **per-category counts** only (no sidebar badge). `SoftDeleteRegistryService` scans `app/Models`, keeps concrete `Model` subclasses using the trait, filters to agency-scoped models for non-owners (owners see all), counts via `onlyTrashed()` (each wrapped so a model whose scope errors is skipped, never fatal). Restore re-fetches under scope (`onlyTrashed()->find` → cross-agency id 404s) and writes a `soft_delete_restorations` audit row (model_type/id/label/agency/by/at). Files: spec, migration+model, service, `Admin\SoftDeleteController`, 2 Blade views, 3 routes, sidebar link + section gate. 5 feature tests green (index render, agency-scoped counts, restore+audit, cross-agency restore denied, unknown-key 404). The integration moat (Template → CdsDraft → blade → merged_html → SurfaceNormalizer → LetterheadRefresher → InsertableBlockRenderer → RoleBlockExpansionService → SigningController → sign.blade.php) is now under test. **Commit 6** shipped the pipeline gate: `scripts/dev-check.ps1` (step 6) fails any commit that changes one of the 10 pipeline files without a matching test diff in `tests/Feature/Docuperfect/SigningView/` (or its supporting `tests/Concerns/BuildsSigningSession.php` + `tests/Fixtures/templates/`). Bypass exists (`-SkipPipelineGate`) for follow-up cleanup commits where the test diff landed previously, but the bypass is documented in CLAUDE.md as never-for-skirting-tests. Verified live: gate fails when a pipeline file is touched without a test diff, passes when changes are isolated. 70 contract tests green (203 assertions). The discipline gap that let B3's 49 unit tests coexist with five live runtime breaks is structurally closed.
- **2026-05-27** — E-sign reset **Commit 5** shipped: source-of-truth collapse for `field_mappings`. New `Template::canonicalFieldMappings()` is the single read site, with three-tier priority (cds_drafts row → editor_state.mappings → legacy field_mappings column). `Template::pruneOrphanFieldMappings()` walks the saved tagged_html + cds_json + editor_state.tags, collects every `tag-…` reference, and removes any field_mappings entry whose tag-id is no longer live — guards against the "blade has 1 seller block but field_mappings has 14" divergence that caused Johan's "save 1 seller, reload 4 sellers" revert. `TemplateController::cdsGenerate` hooks the prune + soft-deletes the applied draft AND older saved drafts for the same `(user, source_template_id)` pair — so the tier-1 lookup falls through cleanly to the freshly-saved editor_state next time. Tests: new `CanonicalFieldMappingsTest` (5 cases — fallback chain, prune behaviour, no-op when no reference source). The full reset's contract suite is now 70 passing (203 assertions): `RealTemplate111EndToEndTest` 7/7 green, plus the 4 sister test files (`ApplyToAllConsentGate`, `OtherConditionsTolerance`, `CanonicalFieldMappings`, plus the 49 pre-existing RecipientLoop tests). Five of six commits landed — Commit 6 (CI gate) closes the discipline regression guard.
- **2026-05-27** — E-sign reset **Commit 4** shipped: OTHER_CONDITIONS three-layer fix. Layer C (regex tolerance): `InsertableBlockRenderer::renderUnboundMarkers()` now uses a permissive match `/~{4,}([^~]{1,200}?)~{4,}/s` + new `normalisePurposeToken()` that strips HTML, normalises case + whitespace, and fuzzy-matches against `CANONICAL_PURPOSE_TOKENS` (Levenshtein ≤ 2). So `~~~~<span>Other Contitions</span>~~~~` (embedded HTML + misspelling, both observed live) resolves to `OTHER_CONDITIONS` rather than rendering literally. Layer B (freshness guard): new `MergedHtmlFreshnessGuard` service compares `template.updated_at` to `document.rendered_at` (falls back to `updated_at` proxy until a migration adds the column); when stale, re-renders the blade view, replaces `merged_html`, logs `merged_html_rerendered` to `SignatureAuditLog`. Wired into `SigningController::show()` so the signing pipeline never serves a stale snapshot when the template was edited after the document. Layer A (builder validator): CDS builder `_doSaveDraft()` runs `_validateMarkerTokens()` on the tagged HTML pre-save; same pipeline as the server (strip HTML, normalise, fuzzy match) and surfaces warnings on Alpine `markerWarnings` state. Doesn't block save (agent might legitimately use a CUSTOM token) but flags malformed cases for cleanup. New test file `OtherConditionsToleranceTest` (6 cases) + the existing `RealTemplate111EndToEndTest::test_malformed_other_conditions_marker_does_not_render_literally` flipped RED → GREEN. 52 regression tests still pass (158 assertions). Closes Q3 of `.ai/audits/esign-reset-investigation-2026-05-27.md`.
- **2026-05-27** — E-sign reset **Commit 3** shipped: multi-cluster bailout fix (largest-cluster-wins). `RoleBlockExpansionService::expandWithLooping()` now pre-computes the canonical cluster per role (`resolveCanonicalClusterPerRole`) and only the canonical cluster runs Case A duplication; stray clusters (e.g. opening-paragraph `[Seller Name Surname ID]` references) stamp as `role_1` by convention. `RoleBlockDetectionService` boundary descriptor gained a `field_count` field so the resolver can pick "largest cluster wins" deterministically. The audit Q2 bug — "only seller_1 fields rendered for 3-seller sessions" — is closed: the contract suite's four blocked tests (seller_2/seller_3 render, viewer-editable for seller_2, viewer-static for seller_1) flipped from RED to GREEN against the canonical template-111 fixture. No regressions: 49 existing RecipientLoop tests still green (150 assertions). Trait `BuildsSigningSession::extractRenderedDocumentHtml()` switched from PCRE backtracking (which choked on Blade's `@json` HEX-encoded HTML over ~6K chars) to a byte-by-byte JSON-string walker that respects `\u00XX` and `\\` escape pairs deterministically. The integration moat catches the bug; the fix lands green against the moat.
- **2026-05-27** — E-sign reset **Commit 2** shipped: end-to-end test scaffold + canonical template-111 fixture. Three new files: (1) `tests/Fixtures/templates/template-111-canonical.blade.php` mirroring the live template 111 pathologies (opening-paragraph `[Seller Name Surname ID]` stray + main seller block + both clean `~~~~OTHER_CONDITIONS~~~~` and malformed `~~~~<span>Other Contitions</span>~~~~` markers); (2) `tests/Concerns/BuildsSigningSession.php` trait drives the REAL `SignatureService::createSigningRequest()` path + transitions recipients out of `STATUS_WAITING` so the signing surface renders; (3) `tests/Feature/Docuperfect/SigningView/RealTemplate111EndToEndTest.php` — 7 tests asserting on the rendered HTML decoded from Alpine's `webTemplateHtml` state. Current state: 1 sanity passes, 6 expected failures pinpoint the bugs Commits 3-5 land green against (seller_2/seller_3 render, viewer-editable scope, OTHER_CONDITIONS tolerance, canonical accessor). The integration moat that was zero-tested before B1-B3 now has a contract suite. Tests assert on `$response->getContent()` decoded — never on service method returns.
- **2026-05-27** — E-sign reset **Commit 1** shipped: Apply-to-All consent gate now reads `signingRequest.party_role === 'agent'` ALONE (`SigningController.php:405-419`). Closes the legal bypass identified in the audit Q4: a dispatching agent (authed user with `manage_documents`) opening a recipient's signing token no longer inherits the apply-to-all initials bypass — that token belongs to the recipient, and per-page consent is what renders. New regression test `ApplyToAllConsentGateTest` (3 cases, 8 assertions, all passing) asserts on `isAgent: true|false` in the actual `$response->getContent()`. First of six commits closing the audit's findings.
- **2026-05-27** — E-sign reset investigation; report at `.ai/audits/esign-reset-investigation-2026-05-27.md`. Five live runtime breaks investigated against 49/49 passing tests. Findings: (Q1) template revert — six parallel sources of "what fields exist" (cds_json, editor_state.tags, editor_state.mappings, tagged_html, field_mappings, fields_json, blade_view) with no canonical owner; CDS builder rehydrate at `cds-builder.blade.php:1205-1257` never auto-prunes orphan tag IDs after a block deletion. (Q2) seller blocks absent from rendered HTML, not hidden — Case A multi-cluster bailout at `RoleBlockExpansionService.php:524-542` refuses to duplicate because detector reports 2 clusters (seller_name_surname_id sits in opening paragraph, separated from the seller-address/phone/email cluster); stamps only seller_1. (Q3) `~~~~OTHER_CONDITIONS~~~~` literal — merged_html stored when template was in a different state contains misspelled `~~~~Other Contitions~~~~` with embedded HTML span between tildes; `InsertableBlockRenderer.php:459` regex doesn't tolerate either + stale snapshot is served instead of re-rendered from live blade. (Q4) Apply-to-All bypass — `SigningController.php:411-414` defines `$isAgent` as `(hasPermission('manage_documents') OR party_role==='agent')` so dispatching agent opening a recipient link inherits agent gate; must be `party_role==='agent'` alone. (Q5) tests use hand-crafted fixtures that don't match template 111's shape — `BlockRendererTest`'s Case A fixture has 1 clean cluster, never exercises the bailout path; `EditableScopeTest` skips the rendering pipeline entirely (no merged_html → expandWithLooping → blade render); `InfoPanelTest` is the only feature test that hits `/sign/{token}` but asserts on sidebar substrings, never on `data-recipient-identity`/`data-viewer-editable` in `$response->getContent()`. Systemic discipline gap: integration moat (Template → CdsDraft → blade → WebTemplateData → SurfaceNormalizer → LetterheadRefresher → InsertableBlockRenderer → RoleBlockExpansionService → SigningController → sign.blade.php) has zero tests. Fix sequence proposed: (1) gate Apply-to-All on `party_role` — zero blast radius; (2) end-to-end test scaffold + canonical template-111 fixture BEFORE Q2 fix; (3) fix multi-cluster bailout with largest-cluster-wins or explicit `data-role-block` markers; (4) fix OTHER_CONDITIONS with builder validation + MergedHtmlFreshnessGuard + tolerate-HTML regex; (5) source-of-truth collapse — canonical Template::canonicalFieldMappings() accessor, deprecate parallel storage; (6) CI gate failing any pipeline-touching commit without an end-to-end test diff.
- **2026-05-26** — B3 shipped: per-recipient editable scope at signing + server-side auth + per-recipient item counter + Case D.2 static label fix (B2.5 caveat closed) + left info panel teaching recipients the flow. Recipient loop engine complete: identity (B1) + render (B2.5) + scope (B3). Operating principle enforced: B2.5's known limitation killed in same commit per the standard. Server stamps `data-viewer-editable` per field via `RoleBlockExpansionService::stampViewerEditability()` (recipient-identity match + canonical-role-token in `editable_by`, OR agent path); signing-view JS gates on the attribute, not a name-list. `SigningController::saveWebFields()` re-derives authorisation server-side from `field_mappings`, accepts both legacy flat + new identity-wrapped payload shapes, returns 403 + writes `web_fields_save_denied` audit log on violation (DOM trust eliminated). `_computeWebCounts()` extended with a sixth bucket — empty `[data-viewer-editable]` inputs — so the items-remaining counter is automatically per-recipient. `RoleBlockExpansionService::rewriteCloneLabels()` walks text nodes inside each clone, rewrites indexed source labels ("Seller 2" → "Seller 4") to the target instance via word-boundary regex, skips `<input>/<textarea>/<select>/<option>/<script>/<style>` so user data never gets mangled. `resources/views/docuperfect/signatures/external/_info-panel.blade.php` renders the persistent left rail on `>=1024px` with a 5-step guide (config-driven from `config/docuperfect.signing_guidance`), agent contact card from `template->creator`, and Signing-as block resolved via `Template::roleDisplayLabel`. Three new test files (16 tests, 32 assertions) covering scope/audit/label-rewrite/panel; total RecipientLoop suite now 49 passing (150 assertions).
- **2026-05-26** — B2.5 shipped: role-block auto-loop completed. Single-block templates now duplicate N times for N recipients at render — the V1-deferral from yesterday's B2 commit is closed. Engine extension: `RoleBlockDetectionService::detectBlockBoundaries()` walks the rendered body via DOMDocument, clusters consecutive `data-field` elements by role-base, computes a clean LCA per cluster (walks up when the LCA is the field-leaf itself), and emits boundary descriptors with stable XPath handles. `RoleBlockExpansionService::expandWithLooping()` is the new entry-point: per-boundary it dispatches Case A (single-block + N recipients → clone the LCA N times, mangle `data-field` with `__r{n}` suffix for DOM uniqueness, stamp identity, prepend `<h4 class="recipient-block-header">{Template::roleDisplayLabel(...)}: {signer}</h4>`, pre-fill each clone's spans from the recipient's `contact_id` via a sub-name→column map covering name/id/phone/email/address), Case B (max_idx == N → stamp only, B2 behaviour intact), Case C (single-block + 1 recipient → stamp only, singleton header), Case D.1 (K > N hardcoded → stamp N, orphan-mark K-N), Case D.2 (K < N hardcoded → stamp K, attempt to isolate the idx=K sub-block and auto-duplicate K+1..N; falls back to stamp+warning when the per-instance subtree can't be isolated). Wired into `SigningController::show()` replacing `stampIdentities()`. 21 tests passing (9 new B2.5 cases — A/B/C/D.1/D.2, DOM uniqueness, per-instance prefill, mixed-role isolation, rentals labels). Tinker walk against template 347 (4-block hardcoded + 2 sellers): identical output to yesterday's B2 baseline (Case D.1 path, no duplication). Architecture matches the locked spec — agency authors ONE role block, engine loops; hardcoded numbered templates continue to render unchanged. Known limitation: Case D.2 clones retain static index labels from the source block (e.g. an inner `<h4>Seller 2</h4>` clones to "Seller 4" instance verbatim); structural warning surfaces it. B3 (per-recipient editable scope) is next.
- **2026-05-26** — B1 shipped: indexed recipient identity. `role_index` column added to `signature_requests` (NOT `signature_template_recipients` — B0 had table name wrong; corrected in commit message) with PHP-regex backfill that split 84 `seller_2` rows into clean `seller` + role_index=2. `SignatureRequest` model gains `role_identity` accessor + `forRoleInstance(role, idx)` scope. `Template::mapSigningPartyKeys()` extended to auto-number duplicates while leaving singletons unchanged (backward compat). New `Template::roleDisplayLabel()` per-token helper recognises wizard's raw tokens (`seller`/`lessor`/`landlord`/`tenant`) in addition to canonical `owner_party`/`acquiring_party`. Wizard's `:1924-1937` keeps the legacy suffixed party_key string for 8 downstream callers but `SignatureService::createSigningRequest()` splits the suffix at insert so the persisted column is always clean. `SigningController::show()` now exposes `$currentRecipient` + `$currentRoleIdentity` to the view (foundation for B2 renderer + B3 signing scope). 13 tests passing. Tinker walk against live session 249 confirmed Johan→agent_1, James→seller_1, Steve→seller_2.
- **2026-05-26** — Fix A shipped: Step 5 chip rendering now iterates the full `editable_by` array. `ESignWizardController::buildFieldsFromMappings()` preserves the array as `editableBy` payload; `assignedTo` retained as legacy first-of-array string for 8 JS call sites. wizard.blade.php gains `fieldRoleTokens(f)` + `isCreatorRole(role)` helpers; chip render replaced with `<template x-for>` loop. 5 tests passing.
